    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.

             \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}column}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{min}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}column}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{25}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.5}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{IQR}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{\PYZam{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}column}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{max}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}column}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{75}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.5}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{IQR}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{no outlier for column}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{column}\PY{p}{)}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}141}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}the code is modified from https://www.jianshu.com/p/2aad8205738c }
          \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{numpy} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{np}
          \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{semi\PYZus{}supervised} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{LabelPropagation}
          \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{accuracy\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{f1\PYZus{}score}
          \PY{n}{x\PYZus{}semi} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{DATA\PYZus{}numerical\PYZus{}semi}
          \PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x\PYZus{}semi}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{target}
          \PY{n}{x\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}semi}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{DATA\PYZus{}numerical\PYZus{}semi}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{drop}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{target}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{reg}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{RandomState}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}unlabeled\PYZus{}points} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{reg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{rand}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x\PYZus{}semi}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}random\PYZus{}unlabeled\PYZus{}points = random\PYZus{}unlabeled\PYZus{}points}
          \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{random\PYZus{}unlabeled\PYZus{}points}\PY{p}{]} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}the label before delete the labels}
          \PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{random\PYZus{}unlabeled\PYZus{}points}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{=}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} make these labels become unlabeled data}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Unlabeled Number:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{count}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{n}{semi\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{LabelPropagation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{semi\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}semi}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{semi\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}semi}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{random\PYZus{}unlabeled\PYZus{}points}\PY{p}{]} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} predict the unlabeled data}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{accuracy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{accuracy\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
